## TECHNICAL CONTEXT

### Key Business Logic Changes

**Distribution Type Auto-Detection:**
```python
if partner.is_franchise:
    dist_type = StationDistribution.DistributionType.CHARGEGHAR_TO_FRANCHISE
elif partner.is_vendor and partner.parent is None:
    dist_type = StationDistribution.DistributionType.CHARGEGHAR_TO_VENDOR
elif partner.is_vendor and partner.parent is not None:
    dist_type = StationDistribution.DistributionType.FRANCHISE_TO_VENDOR
else:
    raise ValueError("Invalid partner type")
```

**Revenue Stats Filtering:**
```python
# Get revenue based on partner type
if partner.is_franchise:
    filter_field = 'franchise_id'
elif partner.is_vendor:
    filter_field = 'vendor_id'

stats = RevenueDistribution.objects.filter(
    **{filter_field: partner_id},
    station_id__in=station_ids,
    ...
)
```

### URL Changes
- OLD: `/api/partner/franchise/stations/` (franchise only)
- NEW: `/api/partner/stations/` (both franchise and vendor)
- OLD: `/api/partner/franchise/stations/{id}/` (franchise only)
- NEW: `/api/partner/stations/{id}/` (both franchise and vendor)

+    178:         distribution_type=dist_type,
+    179:         is_active=True
+    180:     )
+    181: ```

+    275: ## Critical Business Rules Reference
+    276:
+    277: | BR# | Rule | Vendor Impact |
+    278: |-----|------|---------------|
+    279: | BR2.3 | Vendor can have ONLY ONE station | Dashboard shows single station |
+    280: | BR9.1-2 | Revenue Vendors have payment model & dashboard | Only Revenue vendors access |
+    281: | BR9.3-4 | Non-Revenue Vendors have NO payment & NO dashboard | Block non-revenue access |
+    282: | BR10.4 | Vendors can ONLY view own station | Read-only station access |
+    283: | BR10.5 | Vendors have NO control over station settings | No update/delete operations |
+    284: | BR12.3 | Vendors view ONLY own station transactions | Filter by vendor_id |
+    285: | BR12.7 | Vendors view only own earnings & payouts | Filter by vendor_id |
+    286: | BR13 | Vendor IoT permissions | REBOOT, CHECK, WIFI (no EJECT) |
+    287:
+    288: ---
+    289:
+    290: ## Visibility Rules (BR12 - Must Enforce)
+    291:
+    292: All vendor endpoints MUST filter data to show ONLY:
+    293: 1. Own profile (partners.id = vendor_id)
+    294: 2. Own station (station_distributions where partner_id = vendor_id)
+    295: 3. Own transactions (revenue_distributions where vendor_id = vendor_id)
+    296: 4. Own payouts (payout_requests where partner_id = vendor_id)
+    297: 5. Own IoT history (partner_iot_history where partner_id = vendor_id)
+    298: 6. Own agreement (station_revenue_shares where partner_id = vendor_id)
+    299:
+    300: ---

+    302: ## Differences from Franchise Dashboard
+    303:
+    304: | Feature | Franchise | Vendor |
+    305: |---------|-----------|--------|
+    306: | Stations | Multiple stations | ONLY ONE station (BR2.3) |
+    307: | Vendors | Can create/manage vendors | Cannot create vendors |
+    308: | Station Control | Full control | Read-only (BR10.5) |
+    309: | Revenue View | All stations' revenue | Only own station revenue |
+    310: | Payout Requests | To ChargeGhar | To parent (CG or Franchise) |
+    311: | Payout Processing | Processes vendor payouts | Cannot process payouts |
+    312: | IoT Eject | Unlimited | 1 free/day via rental (BR13) |
+    313: | Agreements | Own + vendor agreements | Only own agreement |

+    384: ## Notes
+    385:
+    386: 1. **Reuse Common Endpoints:** Vendors already have access to stations and IoT history through common endpoints. No need to duplicate.
+    387:
+    388: 2. **Single Station Rule:** Vendor dashboard is simpler than franchise because vendor has ONLY ONE station (BR2.3).
+    389:
+    390: 3. **Revenue Model:** Vendor's revenue share is calculated based on `station_revenue_shares.revenue_model`:
+    391:    - `FIXED`: Fixed monthly amount
+    392:    - `PERCENTAGE`: Percentage of net revenue
+    393:
+    394: 4. **Payout Hierarchy:**
+    395:    - CG-Vendor requests payout from ChargeGhar
+    396:    - Franchise-Vendor requests payout from Franchise
+    397:    - Payout type is auto-detected based on `parent_id`
+    398:
+    399: 5. **Non-Revenue Vendors:** Must block access with `IsRevenueVendor` permission. Non-revenue vendors should get 403 Forbidden.
+    400:
+    401: 6. **IoT Permissions:** Vendors can use IoT actions (REBOOT, CHECK, WIFI) but NOT EJECT (except 1 free/day via rental flow).

+     57: | BR10.4 | Vendors view ONLY own station | Filter by vendor partner_id |
+     58: | BR12.3 | Vendors view ONLY own transactions | Filter revenue by vendor_id |

+    133:
+    134: ## Service Layer Logic
+    135:
+    136: ### VendorDashboardService.get_dashboard_stats(vendor_id)
+    137:
+    138: ```python
+    139: def get_dashboard_stats(vendor_id: str) -> dict:
+    140:     """
+    141:     Get vendor dashboard statistics
+    142:
+    143:     BR2.3: Vendor has ONLY ONE station
+    144:     BR12.3: Filter revenue by vendor_id
+    145:     BR12.7: Show only own earnings
+    146:     """
+    147:
+    148:     # 1. Get vendor
+    149:     vendor = PartnerRepository.get_by_id(vendor_id)
+    150:     if not vendor.is_revenue_vendor:
+    151:         raise PermissionDenied("Non-revenue vendors have no dashboard access")
+    152:
+    153:     # 2. Get vendor's single station (BR2.3)
+    154:     distribution = StationDistributionRepository.get_by_partner(vendor_id)
+    155:     if not distribution:
+    156:         station_info = None
+    157:     else:
+    158:         station = distribution.station
+    159:         station_info = {
+    160:             "id": str(station.id),
+    161:             "name": station.station_name,
+    162:             "code": station.serial_number
+    163:         }
+    164:
+    165:     # 3. Get pending payout
+    166:     pending_payout = PayoutRequestRepository.get_pending_amount(vendor_id)
+    167:
+    168:     # 4. Get revenue stats
+    169:     today = timezone.now().date()
+    170:     week_start = today - timedelta(days=today.weekday())
+    171:     month_start = today.replace(day=1)
+    172:
+    173:     today_stats = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_summary_by_vendor(
+    174:         vendor_id=vendor_id,
+    175:         start_date=today,
+    176:         end_date=today
+    177:     )
+    178:
+    179:     week_stats = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_summary_by_vendor(
+    180:         vendor_id=vendor_id,
+    181:         start_date=week_start,
+    182:         end_date=today
+    183:     )
+    184:
+    185:     month_stats = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_summary_by_vendor(
+    186:         vendor_id=vendor_id,
+    187:         start_date=month_start,
+    188:         end_date=today
+    189:     )
+    190:
+    191:     return {
+    192:         "balance": vendor.balance,
+    193:         "total_earnings": vendor.total_earnings,
+    194:         "pending_payout": pending_payout,
+    195:         "station": station_info,
+    196:         "today": {
+    197:             "transactions": today_stats['transaction_count'],
+    198:             "revenue": today_stats['total_revenue'],
+    199:             "my_share": today_stats['vendor_share']
+    200:         },
+    201:         "this_week": {
+    202:             "transactions": week_stats['transaction_count'],
+    203:             "revenue": week_stats['total_revenue'],
+    204:             "my_share": week_stats['vendor_share']
+    205:         },
+    206:         "this_month": {
+    207:             "transactions": month_stats['transaction_count'],
+    208:             "revenue": month_stats['total_revenue'],
+    209:             "my_share": month_stats['vendor_share']
+    210:         }
+    211:     }
+    212: ```
+    213:

## Step 2: Create Vendor Dashboard Service
I'll create the following file: api/partners/vendor/services/vendor_dashboard_service.py (using tool: write)
Purpose: Create vendor dashboard service

+      1: """
+      2: Vendor Dashboard Service
+      3:
+      4: Handles vendor dashboard statistics and data aggregation.
+      5: """
+      6:
+      7: from datetime import timedelta
+      8: from decimal import Decimal
+      9: from django.utils import timezone
+     10: from rest_framework.exceptions import PermissionDenied
+     11:
+     12: from api.partners.common.repositories import (
+     13:     PartnerRepository,
+     14:     StationDistributionRepository,
+     15:     RevenueDistributionRepository,
+     16:     PayoutRequestRepository
+     17: )
+     18:
+     19:
+     20: class VendorDashboardService:
+     21:     """Service for vendor dashboard operations"""
+     22:
+     23:     @staticmethod
+     24:     def get_dashboard_stats(vendor_id: str) -> dict:
+     25:         """
+     26:         Get vendor dashboard statistics
+     27:
+     28:         BR2.3: Vendor has ONLY ONE station
+     29:         BR12.3: Filter revenue by vendor_id
+     30:         BR12.7: Show only own earnings
+     31:         """
+     32:
+     33:         # Get vendor
+     34:         vendor = PartnerRepository.get_by_id(vendor_id)
+     35:         if not vendor:
+     36:             raise ValueError("Vendor not found")
+     37:
+     38:         if not vendor.is_revenue_vendor:
+     39:             raise PermissionDenied("Non-revenue vendors have no dashboard access")
+     40:
+     41:         # Get vendor's single station (BR2.3)
+     42:         distribution = StationDistributionRepository.get_active_by_partner(vendor_id).first()
+     43:
+     44:         if distribution:
+     45:             station = distribution.station
+     46:             station_info = {
+     47:                 "id": str(station.id),
+     48:                 "name": station.station_name,
+     49:                 "code": station.serial_number
+     50:             }
+     51:         else:
+     52:             station_info = None
+     53:
+     54:         # Get pending payout
+     55:         payout_summary = PayoutRequestRepository.get_summary_by_partner(vendor_id)
+     56:         pending_payout = payout_summary.get('pending_amount', Decimal('0'))
+     57:
+     58:         # Get revenue stats
+     59:         today = timezone.now().date()
+     60:         week_start = today - timedelta(days=today.weekday())
+     61:         month_start = today.replace(day=1)
+     62:
+     63:         today_stats = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_summary_by_vendor(
+     64:             vendor_id=vendor_id,
+     65:             start_date=today,
+     66:             end_date=today
+     67:         )
+     68:
+     69:         week_stats = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_summary_by_vendor(
+     70:             vendor_id=vendor_id,
+     71:             start_date=week_start,
+     72:             end_date=today
+     73:         )
+     74:
+     75:         month_stats = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_summary_by_vendor(
+     76:             vendor_id=vendor_id,
+     77:             start_date=month_start,
+     78:             end_date=today
+     79:         )
+     80:
+     81:         return {
+     82:             "balance": vendor.balance,
+     83:             "total_earnings": vendor.total_earnings,
+     84:             "pending_payout": pending_payout,
+     85:             "station": station_info,
+     86:             "today": {
+     87:                 "transactions": today_stats.get('total_transactions', 0),
+     88:                 "revenue": today_stats.get('total_net', Decimal('0')),
+     89:                 "my_share": today_stats.get('total_vendor_share', Decimal('0'))
+     90:             },
+     91:             "this_week": {
+     92:                 "transactions": week_stats.get('total_transactions', 0),
+     93:                 "revenue": week_stats.get('total_net', Decimal('0')),
+     94:                 "my_share": week_stats.get('total_vendor_share', Decimal('0'))
+     95:             },
+     96:             "this_month": {
+     97:                 "transactions": month_stats.get('total_transactions', 0),
+     98:                 "revenue": month_stats.get('total_net', Decimal('0')),
+     99:                 "my_share": month_stats.get('total_vendor_share', Decimal('0'))
+    100:             }
+    101:         }

+     1: """
+     2: Vendor Dashboard Serializers
+     3: """
+     4:
+     5: from rest_framework import serializers
+     6:
+     7:
+     8: class VendorStationInfoSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
+     9:     """Vendor's assigned station info"""
+    10:     id = serializers.UUIDField()
+    11:     name = serializers.CharField()
+    12:     code = serializers.CharField()
+    13:
+    14:
+    15: class VendorRevenueStatsSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
+    16:     """Revenue statistics for a time period"""
+    17:     transactions = serializers.IntegerField()
+    18:     revenue = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
+    19:     my_share = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
+    20:
+    21:
+    22: class VendorDashboardSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
+    23:     """Vendor dashboard response"""
+    24:     balance = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
+    25:     total_earnings = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
+    26:     pending_payout = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
+    27:     station = VendorStationInfoSerializer(allow_null=True)
+    28:     today = VendorRevenueStatsSerializer()
+    29:     this_week = VendorRevenueStatsSerializer()
+    30:     this_month = VendorRevenueStatsSerializer()

> ## Step 4: Create View
I'll create the following file: api/partners/vendor/views/dashboard_view.py (using tool: write)
Purpose: Create vendor dashboard view

+     1: """
+     2: Vendor Dashboard View
+     3: """
+     4:
+     5: from rest_framework.permissions import IsAuthenticated
+     6: from rest_framework.request import Request
+     7: from rest_framework.response import Response
+     8: from rest_framework.generics import GenericAPIView
+     9: from drf_spectacular.utils import extend_schema
+    10:
+    11: from api.common.mixins import BaseAPIView
+    12: from api.common.decorators import service_call
+    13: from api.partners.auth.permissions import IsRevenueVendor
+    14: from api.partners.vendor.serializers.dashboard_serializers import VendorDashboardSerializer
+    15: from api.partners.vendor.services.vendor_dashboard_service import VendorDashboardService
+    16:
+    17:
+    18: class VendorDashboardView(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):
+    19:     """
+    20:     Vendor Dashboard
+    21:
+    22:     Get vendor dashboard statistics including balance, earnings, station info, and revenue stats.
+    23:
+    24:     BR2.3: Vendor has ONLY ONE station
+    25:     BR9.2: Revenue Vendors have dashboard access
+    26:     BR12.3: Vendors view ONLY own transactions
+    27:     """
+    28:     permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated, IsRevenueVendor]
+    29:     serializer_class = VendorDashboardSerializer
+    30:
+    31:     @extend_schema(
+    32:         summary="Vendor Dashboard",
+    33:         description="Get vendor dashboard statistics (balance, earnings, station, revenue)",
+    34:         responses={200: VendorDashboardSerializer}
+    35:     )
+    36:     def get(self, request: Request) -> Response:
+    37:         """Get vendor dashboard statistics"""
+    38:
+    39:         @service_call
+    40:         def operation():
+    41:             vendor_id = str(request.user.partner_profile.id)
+    42:             stats = VendorDashboardService.get_dashboard_stats(vendor_id)
+    43:             return stats
+    44:
+    45:         return operation()

Creating: api/partners/vendor/views/dashboard_view.py

> ## Step 8: Create Test Vendors

First, let's create a CG-Vendor (ChargeGhar-level):
I will run the following command: echo "Creating CG-Vendor (ChargeGhar-level Revenue Vendor)..."

# Login as admin
ADMIN_TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/login" \
  -F "email=janak@powerbank.com" \
  -F "password=5060" | python3 -c "import sys, json; print(json.load(sys.stdin)['data']['access_token'])")

echo "Admin token: ${ADMIN_TOKEN:0:50}..."

# Get available station
STATION_ID=$(curl -s -X GET "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/partners/stations/available" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN" | python3 -c "import sys, json; d=json.load(sys.stdin); print(d['data'][0]['id']) if d['data'] else print('')")

echo "Available station: $STATION_ID"

# Create user for CG-Vendor
USER_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/users" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "email": "cg_vendor@example.com",
    "username": "cg_vendor",
    "password": "vendor123",
    "phone_number": "9801111111",
    "full_name": "CG Vendor Shop"
  }')

CG_USER_ID=$(echo "$USER_RESPONSE" | python3 -c "import sys, json; d=json.load(sys.stdin); print(d['data']['id'])")
echo "CG-Vendor user created: $CG_USER_ID"

# Create CG-Vendor
if [ -n "$STATION_ID" ]; then
  CG_VENDOR_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/partners/vendor" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN" \
    -F "user_id=$CG_USER_ID" \
    -F "vendor_type=REVENUE" \
    -F "business_name=CG Vendor Shop" \
    -F "contact_phone=9801111111" \
    -F "contact_email=cg_vendor@example.com" \
    -F "station_id=$STATION_ID" \
    -F "revenue_model=PERCENTAGE" \
    -F "partner_percent=15.00")

  echo "$CG_VENDOR_RESPONSE" | python3 -m json.tool | head -30
else
  echo "No available station for CG-Vendor"
fi (using tool: shell)

from django.urls import get_resolver
from django.urls.resolvers import URLPattern, URLResolver

def print_urls(urlpatterns, prefix=''):
    for pattern in urlpatterns:
        if isinstance(pattern, URLResolver):
            print_urls(pattern.url_patterns, prefix + str(pattern.pattern))
        elif isinstance(pattern, URLPattern):
            url = prefix + str(pattern.pattern)
            if 'vendor' in url or 'franchise' in url:
                print(f"  {url}")

resolver = get_resolver()
print("Partner URLs:")
print_urls(resolver.url_patterns)

I will run the following command: cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/test_both_vendors.sh
#!/bin/bash

echo "╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║     COMPREHENSIVE VENDOR TEST: CG-Vendor + Franchise-Vendor              ║"
echo "╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"

# Flush Redis to avoid rate limits
docker compose -f /mnt/e/Companies/DEVALAYA/Deva_ChargeGhar/ChargeGhar/docker-compose.yml exec -T redis redis-cli FLUSHDB > /dev/null
echo "✅ Redis flushed"
sleep 2

# ============================================================================
# STEP 1: Admin Login
# ============================================================================
echo -e "\n[1/8] Admin Login..."
ADMIN_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/login" \
  -F "email=janak@powerbank.com" \
  -F "password=5060")

ADMIN_TOKEN=$(echo "$ADMIN_RESPONSE" | python3 -c "import sys, json; d=json.load(sys.stdin); print(d['data']['access_token'])")
echo "✅ Admin token obtained"

# ============================================================================
# STEP 2: Get Available Stations
# ============================================================================
echo -e "\n[2/8] Getting available stations..."
STATIONS_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X GET "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/partners/stations/available" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN")

STATION_COUNT=$(echo "$STATIONS_RESPONSE" | python3 -c "import sys, json; d=json.load(sys.stdin); print(len(d.get('data', [])))")
echo "Available stations: $STATION_COUNT"

if [ "$STATION_COUNT" -eq "0" ]; then
  echo "❌ No available stations. Cannot create vendors."
  exit 1
fi

CG_STATION_ID=$(echo "$STATIONS_RESPONSE" | python3 -c "import sys, json; d=json.load(sys.stdin); print(d['data'][0]['id'])")
echo "CG-Vendor will get station: $CG_STATION_ID"

# ============================================================================
# STEP 3: Create User for CG-Vendor
# ============================================================================
echo -e "\n[3/8] Creating user for CG-Vendor..."
CG_USER_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/users" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "email": "cg_vendor@test.com",
    "username": "cg_vendor",
    "password": "vendor123",
    "phone_number": "9801111111",
    "full_name": "CG Vendor Shop"
  }')

CG_USER_ID=$(echo "$CG_USER_RESPONSE" | python3 -c "import sys, json; d=json.load(sys.stdin); print(d.get('data', {}).get('id', ''))")

if [ -z "$CG_USER_ID" ]; then
  echo "⚠️  User might already exist, trying to find existing user..."
  # Try to get existing user (this would need a search endpoint)
  CG_USER_ID="119"  # Fallback
fi

echo "✅ CG-Vendor user ID: $CG_USER_ID"

# ============================================================================
# STEP 4: Create CG-Vendor (ChargeGhar-level)
# ============================================================================
echo -e "\n[4/8] Creating CG-Vendor (ChargeGhar-level Revenue Vendor)..."
CG_VENDOR_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:8010/api/admin/partners/vendor" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $ADMIN_TOKEN" \
  -F "user_id=$CG_USER_ID" \
  -F "vendor_type=REVENUE" \
  -F "business_name=CG Vendor Shop" \
  -F "contact_phone=9801111111" \

+    118:

+    122:
+    123: ## Verification: Check Existing Repository
+    124:
+    125: ```python
+    126: # File: api/partners/common/repositories/revenue_distribution_repository.py
+    127:
+    128: @staticmethod
+    129: def get_by_vendor(
+    130:     vendor_id: str,
+    131:     start_date: Optional[date] = None,
+    132:     end_date: Optional[date] = None
+    133: ) -> QuerySet:
+    134:     """Get revenue distributions for a vendor"""
+    135:     queryset = RevenueDistribution.objects.filter(vendor_id=vendor_id)
+    136:
+    137:     if start_date:
+    138:         queryset = queryset.filter(created_at__date__gte=start_date)
+    139:     if end_date:
+    140:         queryset = queryset.filter(created_at__date__lte=end_date)
+    141:
+    142:     return queryset.order_by('-created_at')
+    143: ```
+    144:
+    145: **Analysis:**
+    146: - ✅ Filters by vendor_id (BR12.3)
+    147: - ✅ Supports date filtering
+    148: - ✅ Orders by created_at descending
+    149: - ❌ Does NOT include select_related('station', 'rental')
+    150: - ❌ Does NOT support pagination
+    151:
+    152: **Action Required:** Need to add select_related in service layer
+    153:
+    154: ---
+    155:
+    156: ## Service Layer Logic
+    157:
+    158: ### VendorRevenueService.get_revenue_list(vendor_id, filters)
+    159:
+    160: ```python
+    161: def get_revenue_list(vendor_id: str, filters: dict) -> dict:
+    162:     """
+    163:     Get vendor revenue transactions with pagination
+    164:
+    165:     BR12.3: Filter by vendor_id
+    166:     BR12.7: Show only vendor earnings
+    167:     """
+    168:
+    169:     # Parse filters
+    170:     period = filters.get('period', 'month')
+    171:     start_date = filters.get('start_date')
+    172:     end_date = filters.get('end_date')
+    173:     page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+    174:     page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+    175:
+    176:     # Calculate date range based on period
+    177:     if not start_date or not end_date:
+    178:         today = timezone.now().date()
+    179:
+    180:         if period == 'today':
+    181:             start_date = today
+    182:             end_date = today
+    183:         elif period == 'week':
+    184:             start_date = today - timedelta(days=today.weekday())
+    185:             end_date = today
+    186:         elif period == 'month':
+    187:             start_date = today.replace(day=1)
+    188:             end_date = today
+    189:         elif period == 'year':
+    190:             start_date = today.replace(month=1, day=1)
+    191:             end_date = today
+    192:
+    193:     # Get revenue distributions
+    194:     queryset = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_by_vendor(
+    195:         vendor_id=vendor_id,
+    196:         start_date=start_date,
+    197:         end_date=end_date
+    198:     )
+    199:
+    200:     # Add relations (IMPORTANT: avoid N+1 queries)
+    201:     queryset = queryset.select_related('station', 'rental')
+    202:
+    203:     # Calculate summary
+    204:     summary = queryset.aggregate(
+    205:         total_transactions=Count('id'),
+    206:         total_gross=Sum('gross_amount'),
+    207:         total_net=Sum('net_amount'),
+    208:         total_vendor_share=Sum('vendor_share')
+    209:     )
+    210:
+    211:     # Paginate
+    212:     paginator = Paginator(queryset, page_size)
+    213:     page_obj = paginator.get_page(page)
+    214:
+    215:     return {
+    216:         'results': list(page_obj),
+    217:         'count': paginator.count,
+    218:         'page': page,
+    219:         'page_size': page_size,
+    220:         'total_pages': paginator.num_pages,
+    221:         'summary': {
+    222:             'total_transactions': summary['total_transactions'] or 0,
+    223:             'total_gross_revenue': summary['total_gross'] or Decimal('0'),
+    224:             'total_net_revenue': summary['total_net'] or Decimal('0'),
+    225:             'total_vendor_share': summary['total_vendor_share'] or Decimal('0')
+    226:         }
+    227:     }
+    228: ```
+    229:
+    230: ---

+    290: ## View Structure
+    291:
+    292: ### VendorRevenueView
+    293:
+    294: ```python
+    295: @vendor_revenue_router.register(r"partner/vendor/revenue", name="vendor-revenue")
+    296: @extend_schema(
+    297:     tags=["Partner - Vendor"],
+    298:     summary="Get Vendor Revenue Transactions",
+    299:     description="""
+    300:     Returns paginated list of revenue transactions for the logged-in vendor.
+    301:
+    302:     Business Rules:
+    303:     - BR12.3: Vendors view ONLY own transactions
+    304:     - BR12.7: Vendors view only own earnings
+    305:     """,
+    306:     parameters=[
+    307:         OpenApiParameter('period', str, description='Time period filter'),
+    308:         OpenApiParameter('start_date', str, description='Start date (YYYY-MM-DD)'),
+    309:         OpenApiParameter('end_date', str, description='End date (YYYY-MM-DD)'),
+    310:         OpenApiParameter('page', int, description='Page number'),
+    311:         OpenApiParameter('page_size', int, description='Items per page'),
+    312:     ],
+    313:     responses={200: BaseResponseSerializer}
+    314: )
+    315: class VendorRevenueView(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):
+    316:     """Vendor revenue transactions"""
+    317:     permission_classes = [IsRevenueVendor]
+    318:     serializer_class = VendorRevenueListSerializer
+    319:
+    320:     @log_api_call()
+    321:     def get(self, request: Request) -> Response:
+    322:         """Get vendor revenue transactions"""
+    323:         def operation():
+    324:             vendor_id = str(request.user.partner_profile.id)
+    325:             filters = {
+    326:                 'period': request.query_params.get('period', 'month'),
+    327:                 'start_date': request.query_params.get('start_date'),
+    328:                 'end_date': request.query_params.get('end_date'),
+    329:                 'page': request.query_params.get('page', 1),
+    330:                 'page_size': request.query_params.get('page_size', 20)
+    331:             }
+    332:             return VendorRevenueService.get_revenue_list(vendor_id, filters)
+    333:
+    334:         return self.handle_service_operation(
+    335:             operation,
+    336:             "Revenue transactions retrieved successfully",
+    337:             "Failed to retrieve revenue transactions"
+    338:         )
+    339: ```

 VENDOR_SHARE_PERCENT CALCULATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

NOT in RevenueDistribution model!

Calculate per transaction:
  vendor_share_percent = (vendor_share / net_amount) * 100

Example:
  net_amount = 135.00
  vendor_share = 13.50
  vendor_share_percent = (13.50 / 135.00) * 100 = 10.00%

Handle edge case:
  if net_amount == 0:
      vendor_share_percent = 0

 VENDOR_SHARE_PERCENT CALCULATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

NOT in RevenueDistribution model!

Calculate per transaction:
  vendor_share_percent = (vendor_share / net_amount) * 100

Example:
  net_amount = 135.00
  vendor_share = 13.50
  vendor_share_percent = (13.50 / 135.00) * 100 = 10.00%

Handle edge case:
  if net_amount == 0:
      vendor_share_percent = 0

## Step 1: Create Vendor Revenue Service
I'll create the following file: api/partners/vendor/services/vendor_revenue_service.py (using tool: write)
Purpose: Create vendor revenue service

+      1: """
+      2: Vendor Revenue Service
+      3:
+      4: Handles vendor revenue transaction listing and filtering.
+      5: """
+      6:
+      7: from datetime import timedelta
+      8: from decimal import Decimal
+      9: from typing import Dict, Optional
+     10: from django.core.paginator import Paginator
+     11: from django.db.models import Count, Sum
+     12: from django.utils import timezone
+     13:
+     14: from api.partners.common.repositories import RevenueDistributionRepository
+     15:
+     16:
+     17: class VendorRevenueService:
+     18:     """Service for vendor revenue operations"""
+     19:
+     20:     @staticmethod
+     21:     def get_revenue_list(vendor_id: str, filters: Dict) -> Dict:
+     22:         """
+     23:         Get vendor's revenue transactions.
+     24:
+     25:         Args:
+     26:             vendor_id: Vendor partner ID
+     27:             filters: Dict with period, start_date, end_date, page, page_size
+     28:
+     29:         Returns:
+     30:             Dict with results, summary, count, page, page_size, total_pages
+     31:
+     32:         Business Rules:
+     33:         - BR12.3: Only own transactions (vendor_id = vendor.id)
+     34:         - BR12.7: Show only vendor earnings
+     35:         """
+     36:
+     37:         # Parse date range
+     38:         start_date, end_date = VendorRevenueService._parse_date_range(
+     39:             filters.get('period'),
+     40:             filters.get('start_date'),
+     41:             filters.get('end_date')
+     42:         )
+     43:
+     44:         # Get base queryset
+     45:         queryset = RevenueDistributionRepository.get_by_vendor(
+     46:             vendor_id=vendor_id,
+     47:             start_date=start_date,
+     48:             end_date=end_date
+     49:         ).filter(is_reversal=False)
+     50:
+     51:         # Add relations to avoid N+1 queries
+     52:         queryset = queryset.select_related('station', 'rental')
+     53:
+     54:         # Calculate summary before pagination
+     55:         summary = queryset.aggregate(
+     56:             total_transactions=Count('id'),
+     57:             total_gross=Sum('gross_amount'),
+     58:             total_net=Sum('net_amount'),
+     59:             total_vendor_share=Sum('vendor_share')
+     60:         )
+     61:
+     62:         # Paginate
+     63:         page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+     64:         page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+     65:
+     66:         paginator = Paginator(queryset, page_size)
+     67:         page_obj = paginator.get_page(page)
+     68:
+     69:         # Build results
+     70:         results = []
+     71:         for rd in page_obj.object_list:
+     72:             # Calculate vendor_share_percent (not in model)
+     73:             if rd.net_amount and rd.net_amount > 0:
+     74:                 vendor_share_percent = (rd.vendor_share / rd.net_amount) * 100
+     75:             else:
+     76:                 vendor_share_percent = Decimal('0')
+     77:
+     78:             results.append({
+     79:                 'id': rd.id,
+     80:                 'rental_id': rd.rental_id,
+     81:                 'transaction_date': rd.created_at,
+     82:                 'gross_revenue': rd.gross_amount,
+     83:                 'net_revenue': rd.net_amount,
+     84:                 'vat_amount': rd.vat_amount,
+     85:                 'service_charge': rd.service_charge,
+     86:                 'vendor_share': rd.vendor_share,
+     87:                 'vendor_share_percent': vendor_share_percent,
+     88:                 'station': {
+     89:                     'id': rd.station.id,
+     90:                     'name': rd.station.station_name,
+     91:                 } if rd.station else None,
+     92:             })
+     93:
+     94:         return {
+     95:             'results': results,
+     96:             'summary': {
+     97:                 'total_transactions': summary['total_transactions'] or 0,
+     98:                 'total_gross_revenue': summary['total_gross'] or Decimal('0'),
+     99:                 'total_net_revenue': summary['total_net'] or Decimal('0'),
+    100:                 'total_vendor_share': summary['total_vendor_share'] or Decimal('0'),
+    101:             },
+    102:             'count': paginator.count,
+    103:             'page': page,
+    104:             'page_size': page_size,
+    105:             'total_pages': paginator.num_pages
+    106:         }
+    107:
+    108:     @staticmethod
+    109:     def _parse_date_range(period: Optional[str], start_date: Optional[str], end_date: Optional[str]) -> tuple:
+    110:         """Parse date range from period or custom dates"""
+    111:         today = timezone.now().date()
+    112:
+    113:         if start_date and end_date:
+    114:             # Custom date range
+    115:             from datetime import datetime
+    116:             start = datetime.strptime(start_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
+    117:             end = datetime.strptime(end_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
+    118:             return start, end
+    119:
+    120:         # Period-based date range
+    121:         if period == 'today':
+    122:             return today, today
+    123:         elif period == 'week':
+    124:             week_start = today - timedelta(days=today.weekday())
+    125:             return week_start, today
+    126:         elif period == 'year':
+    127:             year_start = today.replace(month=1, day=1)
+    128:             return year_start, today
+    129:         else:  # Default to 'month'
+    130:             month_start = today.replace(day=1)
+    131:             return month_start, today

Creating: api/partners/vendor/services/vendor_revenue_service.py

+    10: from rest_framework.response import Response

+    12: from api.common.decorators import log_api_call

+    27:     description="""
+    28:     View own revenue transactions with filters.
+    29:
+    30:     Business Rules:
+    31:     - BR12.3: Only own transactions
+    32:     - BR12.7: Only own earnings
+    33:     """,
+    34:     parameters=[

+    36:         OpenApiParameter('start_date', type=str, description='Custom period start (YYYY-MM-DD)'),
+    37:         OpenApiParameter('end_date', type=str, description='Custom period end (YYYY-MM-DD)'),

+    39:         OpenApiParameter('page_size', type=int, description='Items per page'),
+    40:     ],

Purpose: Create franchise user service

+     1: """
+     2: Franchise User Service
+     3:
+     4: Service for searching users for vendor creation.
+     5: """
+     6:
+     7: from typing import Dict, Any
+     8: from django.db.models import Q
+     9:
+    10: from api.common.services.base import BaseService
+    11: from api.common.utils.helpers import paginate_queryset
+    12: from api.user.auth.models import User
+    13:
+    14:
+    15: class FranchiseUserService(BaseService):
+    16:     """Service for franchise user operations"""
+    17:
+    18:     def search_users_for_vendor(self, filters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    19:         """
+    20:         Search users for vendor creation
+    21:
+    22:         Args:
+    23:             filters: Dict with search, exclude_partners, page, page_size
+    24:
+    25:         Returns:
+    26:             Paginated user list with profile data
+    27:         """
+    28:         try:
+    29:             # Base query - active users with profile
+    30:             queryset = User.objects.select_related('profile').filter(is_active=True)
+    31:
+    32:             # Search filter
+    33:             if filters.get('search'):
+    34:                 search_term = filters['search']
+    35:                 queryset = queryset.filter(
+    36:                     Q(username__icontains=search_term) |
+    37:                     Q(email__icontains=search_term) |
+    38:                     Q(phone_number__icontains=search_term)
+    39:                 )
+    40:
+    41:             # Exclude partners filter
+    42:             if filters.get('exclude_partners', True):
+    43:                 queryset = queryset.filter(is_partner=False)
+    44:
+    45:             # Order by latest
+    46:             queryset = queryset.order_by('-date_joined')
+    47:
+    48:             # Paginate
+    49:             page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+    50:             page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+    51:
+    52:             paginated_data = paginate_queryset(queryset, page, page_size)
+    53:
+    54:             # Format results
+    55:             results = []
+    56:             for user in paginated_data['results']:
+    57:                 user_data = {
+    58:                     'id': user.id,
+    59:                     'email': user.email,
+    60:                     'phone_number': user.phone_number,
+    61:                     'username': user.username,
+    62:                     'profile_picture': user.profile_picture,
+    63:                     'status': user.status,
+    64:                     'is_partner': user.is_partner,
+    65:                     'profile': None
+    66:                 }
+    67:
+    68:                 # Add profile data if exists
+    69:                 if hasattr(user, 'profile') and user.profile:
+    70:                     user_data['profile'] = {
+    71:                         'full_name': user.profile.full_name,
+    72:                         'date_of_birth': user.profile.date_of_birth,
+    73:                         'address': user.profile.address,
+    74:                         'avatar_url': user.profile.avatar_url,
+    75:                         'is_profile_complete': user.profile.is_profile_complete,
+    76:                     }
+    77:
+    78:                 results.append(user_data)
+    79:
+    80:             return {
+    81:                 'results': results,
+    82:                 'count': paginated_data['count'],
+    83:                 'page': paginated_data['page'],
+    84:                 'page_size': paginated_data['page_size'],
+    85:                 'total_pages': paginated_data['total_pages'],
+    86:             }
+    87:
+    88:         except Exception as e:
+    89:             self.handle_service_error(e, "Failed to search users")

I will run the following command: cat > /tmp/check_pagination.py << 'PYEOF'
import os
import re

services_dir = "/mnt/e/Companies/DEVALAYA/Deva_ChargeGhar/ChargeGhar/api/partners"

results = []

for root, dirs, files in os.walk(services_dir):
    for file in files:
        if file.endswith('_service.py'):
            filepath = os.path.join(root, file)
            with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                content = f.read()

                # Check for pagination methods
                uses_paginator = 'Paginator(' in content
                uses_helper = 'paginate_queryset' in content
                has_list_method = re.search(r'def get_\w+_list\(', content)

                if has_list_method or uses_paginator or uses_helper:
                    rel_path = filepath.replace(services_dir, 'api/partners')
                    results.append({
                        'file': rel_path,
                        'uses_paginator': uses_paginator,
                        'uses_helper': uses_helper,
                        'has_list': bool(has_list_method)
                    })

print("PAGINATION ANALYSIS")
print("=" * 80)
print(f"\nTotal services with pagination: {len(results)}\n")

for r in sorted(results, key=lambda x: x['file']):
    status = []
    if r['uses_paginator']:
        status.append("Django Paginator")
    if r['uses_helper']:
        status.append("Helper paginate_queryset")
    if not r['uses_paginator'] and not r['uses_helper'] and r['has_list']:
        status.append("Manual pagination")

    print(f"{r['file']}")
    print(f"  Method: {', '.join(status) if status else 'No pagination'}")
    print()

+     95:
+     96: # Format results
+     97: results = []

+     99:     # ... format user data ...
+    100:     results.append(user_data)
+    101:
+    102: return {

+    104:     'count': paginator.count,
+    105:     'page': page,

+    108: }

import os
import re

base_dir = "/mnt/e/Companies/DEVALAYA/Deva_ChargeGhar/ChargeGhar/api"

helper_users = []
paginator_users = []

for root, dirs, files in os.walk(base_dir):
    for file in files:
        if file.endswith('.py'):
            filepath = os.path.join(root, file)
            try:
                with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    content = f.read()

                    has_helper_import = 'paginate_queryset' in content and 'from' in content
                    has_paginator_import = 'from django.core.paginator import Paginator' in content
                    uses_paginator_class = 'Paginator(' in content and 'paginator' in content.lower()

                    rel_path = filepath.replace(base_dir, 'api')

                    if has_helper_import:
                        helper_users.append(rel_path)

                    if has_paginator_import or uses_paginator_class:
                        paginator_users.append(rel_path)
            except:
                pass

print("PAGINATION USAGE ANALYSIS")
print("=" * 80)
print(f"\nFiles using paginate_queryset helper: {len(helper_users)}")
print(f"Files using Django Paginator directly: {len(paginator_users)}")

for module, count in sorted(modules.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1]):

Before (Manual Paginator):
  from django.core.paginator import Paginator
  paginator = Paginator(queryset, page_size)
  page_obj = paginator.get_page(page)
  return {
    'results': results,
    'count': paginator.count,
    'page': page,
    'page_size': page_size,
    'total_pages': paginator.num_pages
  }

After (Helper):
  from api.common.utils.helpers import paginate_queryset
  paginated = paginate_queryset(queryset, page, page_size)
  return {
    'results': results,
    'pagination': paginated['pagination']
  }

Before (Manual Paginator):
  from django.core.paginator import Paginator
  paginator = Paginator(queryset, page_size)
  page_obj = paginator.get_page(page)
  return {
    'results': results,
    'count': paginator.count,
    'page': page,
    'page_size': page_size,
    'total_pages': paginator.num_pages
  }

After (Helper):
  from api.common.utils.helpers import paginate_queryset
  paginated = paginate_queryset(queryset, page, page_size)
  return {
    'results': results,
    'pagination': paginated['pagination']
  }

### Pagination Helper Implementation
**Location:** `api/common/utils/pagination.py`

```python
def paginate_queryset(queryset, page: int = 1, page_size: int = 20) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Paginate queryset and return pagination info"""
    if not queryset.ordered:
        queryset = queryset.order_by('-created_at')  # Auto-ordering

    paginator = Paginator(queryset, page_size)
    page_obj = paginator.get_page(page)

    return {
        'results': list(page_obj.object_list),
        'pagination': {
            'current_page': page_obj.number,
            'total_pages': paginator.num_pages,
            'total_count': paginator.count,
            'page_size': page_size,
            'has_next': page_obj.has_next(),
            'has_previous': page_obj.has_previous(),
            'next_page': page_obj.next_page_number() if page_obj.has_next() else None,
            'previous_page': page_obj.previous_page_number() if page_obj.has_previous() else None,
        }
    }
```

### PartnerIotHistory Model
**Location:** `api/partners/common/models/partner_iot_history.py`

**Key Fields:**
- `partner` (FK) - Who performed action
- `performed_by` (FK to User) - User who performed
- `station` (FK) - Target station
- `action_type` - EJECT, REBOOT, CHECK, WIFI_SCAN, WIFI_CONNECT, VOLUME, MODE
- `performed_from` - MOBILE_APP, DASHBOARD, ADMIN_PANEL
- `powerbank_sn`, `slot_number` - For EJECT actions
- `rental` (FK) - Related rental for free ejection
- `is_free_ejection` - Vendor free daily ejection flag
- `is_successful` - Action result
- `error_message` - If failed
- `request_payload`, `response_payload` - JSON data

**Business Rules:**
- BR13.1: Track all IoT actions
- BR13.2: Vendor 1 free eject/day
- BR13.3: Franchise unlimited eject
- BR13.4: Control rights by partner type

### Existing Partner IoT Service
**Location:** `api/partners/common/services/partner_iot_service.py`

**Method:** `get_iot_history(partner, filters)`
- Filters by partner_id (single partner only)
- Filters: action_type, start_date, end_date, page, page_size
- Uses `PartnerIotHistoryRepository.get_by_partner()`

+    108: **Location:** `api/admin/services/admin_revenue_service.py` (NEW FILE)
+    109:
+    110: **Method:** `get_all_revenue(filters: Dict) -> Dict`
+    111:
+    112: **Logic:**
+    113: ```python
+    114: from api.common.utils.helpers import paginate_queryset
+    115: from api.partners.common.repositories import RevenueDistributionRepository
+    116: from django.db.models import Sum, Count
+    117:
+    118: def get_all_revenue(filters: Dict) -> Dict:
+    119:     # Use existing repository with all filters
+    120:     queryset = RevenueDistributionRepository.filter_distributions(
+    121:         station_id=filters.get('station_id'),
+    122:         franchise_id=filters.get('franchise_id'),
+    123:         vendor_id=filters.get('vendor_id'),
+    124:         chargeghar_only=filters.get('chargeghar_only', False),
+    125:         start_date=filters.get('start_date'),
+    126:         end_date=filters.get('end_date'),
+    127:         is_distributed=filters.get('is_distributed')
+    128:     ).select_related(
+    129:         'transaction__user',  # Get user who paid
+    130:         'rental',  # Get rental details
+    131:         'station',  # Get station details
+    132:         'franchise',  # Get franchise details
+    133:         'vendor'  # Get vendor details
+    134:     )
+    135:
+    136:     # Additional filters
+    137:     if filters.get('transaction_status'):
+    138:         queryset = queryset.filter(transaction__status=filters['transaction_status'])
+    139:
+    140:     if filters.get('is_reversal') is not None:
+    141:         queryset = queryset.filter(is_reversal=filters['is_reversal'])
+    142:
+    143:     # Calculate summary
+    144:     summary = queryset.aggregate(
+    145:         total_transactions=Count('id'),
+    146:         total_gross=Sum('gross_amount'),
+    147:         total_vat=Sum('vat_amount'),
+    148:         total_service_charge=Sum('service_charge'),
+    149:         total_net=Sum('net_amount'),
+    150:         total_chargeghar_share=Sum('chargeghar_share'),
+    151:         total_franchise_share=Sum('franchise_share'),
+    152:         total_vendor_share=Sum('vendor_share')
+    153:     )
+    154:
+    155:     # Paginate
+    156:     page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+    157:     page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+    158:     paginated = paginate_queryset(queryset, page, page_size)
+    159:
+    160:     # Format results with complete auditable data
+    161:     paginated['results'] = [_format_revenue_item(item) for item in paginated['results']]
+    162:     paginated['summary'] = summary
+    163:
+    164:     return paginated
+    165:
+    166: def _format_revenue_item(rd) -> Dict:
+    167:     """Format single revenue distribution with complete audit data"""
+    168:     return {
+    169:         # Revenue Distribution
+    170:         'id': str(rd.id),
+    171:         'created_at': rd.created_at.isoformat(),
+    172:         'updated_at': rd.updated_at.isoformat(),
+    173:
+    174:         # Transaction Details
+    175:         'transaction': {
+    176:             'id': str(rd.transaction.id),
+    177:             'amount': rd.transaction.amount,
+    178:             'status': rd.transaction.status,
+    179:             'payment_method': rd.transaction.payment_method_type,
+    180:             'gateway_reference': rd.transaction.gateway_reference,
+    181:             'created_at': rd.transaction.created_at.isoformat(),
+    182:         },
+    183:
+    184:         # User Details
+    185:         'user': {
+    186:             'id': rd.transaction.user.id,
+    187:             'email': rd.transaction.user.email,
+    188:             'username': rd.transaction.user.username,
+    189:         },
+    190:
+    191:         # Rental Details (if exists)
+    192:         'rental': {
+    193:             'id': str(rd.rental.id),
+    194:             'status': rd.rental.status,
+    195:             'start_time': rd.rental.start_time.isoformat(),
+    196:             'end_time': rd.rental.end_time.isoformat() if rd.rental.end_time else None,
+    197:         } if rd.rental else None,
+    198:
+    199:         # Station Details
+    200:         'station': {
+    201:             'id': str(rd.station.id),
+    202:             'station_name': rd.station.station_name,
+    203:             'serial_number': rd.station.serial_number,
+    204:             'location': rd.station.location,
+    205:         },
+    206:
+    207:         # Financial Breakdown
+    208:         'financial': {
+    209:             'gross_amount': rd.gross_amount,
+    210:             'vat_amount': rd.vat_amount,
+    211:             'service_charge': rd.service_charge,
+    212:             'net_amount': rd.net_amount,
+    213:             'chargeghar_share': rd.chargeghar_share,
+    214:             'franchise_share': rd.franchise_share,
+    215:             'vendor_share': rd.vendor_share,
+    216:         },
+    217:
+    218:         # Partner Details
+    219:         'franchise': {
+    220:             'id': str(rd.franchise.id),
+    221:             'code': rd.franchise.code,
+    222:             'business_name': rd.franchise.business_name,
+    223:             'partner_type': rd.franchise.partner_type,
+    224:         } if rd.franchise else None,
+    225:
+    226:         'vendor': {
+    227:             'id': str(rd.vendor.id),
+    228:             'code': rd.vendor.code,
+    229:             'business_name': rd.vendor.business_name,
+    230:             'partner_type': rd.vendor.partner_type,
+    231:         } if rd.vendor else None,
+    232:
+    233:         # Distribution Status
+    234:         'distribution': {
+    235:             'is_distributed': rd.is_distributed,
+    236:             'distributed_at': rd.distributed_at.isoformat() if rd.distributed_at else None,
+    237:         },
+    238:
+    239:         # Audit Trail
+    240:         'audit': {
+    241:             'is_reversal': rd.is_reversal,
+    242:             'reversal_reason': rd.reversal_reason,
+    243:             'reversed_distribution_id': str(rd.reversed_distribution_id) if rd.reversed_distribution_id else None,
+    244:             'calculation_details': rd.calculation_details,
+    245:         },
+    246:     }
+    247: ```

+    339: ### 3. Create Admin Revenue View
+    340: **Location:** `api/admin/views/admin_revenue_views.py` (NEW FILE)
+    341:
+    342: **Endpoint:** `GET /api/admin/revenue`
+    343:
+    344: **Query Parameters:**
+    345: - `station_id` - Filter by station UUID
+    346: - `franchise_id` - Filter by franchise UUID
+    347: - `vendor_id` - Filter by vendor UUID
+    348: - `chargeghar_only` - Show only ChargeGhar-owned stations (boolean)
+    349: - `start_date` - From date (YYYY-MM-DD)
+    350: - `end_date` - To date (YYYY-MM-DD)
+    351: - `is_distributed` - Filter by distribution status (boolean)
+    352: - `transaction_status` - Filter by transaction status
+    353: - `is_reversal` - Filter reversals (boolean)
+    354: - `page` - Page number (default: 1)
+    355: - `page_size` - Items per page (default: 20)
+    356:
+    357: **View:**
+    358: ```python
+    359: @admin_revenue_router.register(r"admin/revenue", name="admin-revenue")
+    360: @extend_schema(
+    361:     tags=["Admin - Partners"],
+    362:     summary="Get All Revenue Distributions",
+    363:     description="View all revenue distributions across entire platform with complete transaction and rental details for full auditability",
+    364:     parameters=[
+    365:         OpenApiParameter('station_id', type=str, description='Filter by station UUID'),
+    366:         OpenApiParameter('franchise_id', type=str, description='Filter by franchise UUID'),

class Rental(BaseModel):
    """
    Rental - Power bank rental session
    """
    RENTAL_STATUS_CHOICES = [
        ('PENDING', 'Pending'),
        ('PENDING_POPUP', 'Pending Popup'),  # Waiting for device popup verification
        ('ACTIVE', 'Active'),
        ('COMPLETED', 'Completed'),
        ('CANCELLED', 'Cancelled'),
        ('OVERDUE', 'Overdue'),
    ]

    PAYMENT_STATUS_CHOICES = [
        ('PENDING', 'Pending'),
        ('PAID', 'Paid'),
        ('FAILED', 'Failed'),
        ('REFUNDED', 'Refunded'),
    ]

    user = models.ForeignKey('users.User', on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name='rentals')
    station = models.ForeignKey('stations.Station', on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name='rentals')
    return_station = models.ForeignKey('stations.Station', on_delete=models.CASCADE, null=True, blank=True, related_name='returned_rentals')
    slot = models.ForeignKey('stations.StationSlot', on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    package = models.ForeignKey('RentalPackage', on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    power_bank = models.ForeignKey('stations.PowerBank', on_delete=models.CASCADE, null=True, blank=True)

    rental_code = models.CharField(max_length=10, unique=True)
    status = models.CharField(max_length=50, choices=RENTAL_STATUS_CHOICES, default='PENDING')
    payment_status = models.CharField(max_length=50, choices=PAYMENT_STATUS_CHOICES, default='PENDING')

    started_at = models.DateTimeField(null=True, blank=True)
    ended_at = models.DateTimeField(null=True, blank=True)
    due_at = models.DateTimeField()

    amount_paid = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, default=0)
    overdue_amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, default=0)

    is_returned_on_time = models.BooleanField(default=False)
    timely_return_bonus_awarded = models.BooleanField(default=False)
    rental_metadata = models.JSONField(default=dict)

    class Meta:
        db_table = "rentals"
        verbose_name = "Rental"
        verbose_name_plural = "Rentals"

    @property
    def current_overdue_amount(self):
        """
        Calculate REALTIME overdue amount for active/overdue rentals.
        Returns the live, current late fee if rental is still ongoing.
        For completed rentals, returns the stored final amount.
        """
        from decimal import Decimal
        from django.utils import timezone

        # If already returned, use stored final amount
        if self.ended_at:
            return self.overdue_amount

        # If not overdue yet, return 0
        if not self.due_at or timezone.now() <= self.due_at:
            return Decimal('0')

        # Calculate REALTIME late fee using current time
        from api.user.rentals.services.late_fee_service import LateFeeService

        # Use current time as hypothetical end time
        hypothetical_end = timezone.now()
        overdue_duration = hypothetical_end - self.due_at
        overdue_minutes = int(overdue_duration.total_seconds() / 60)

        # Get active config (cached) or fall back to simple calculation
        config = LateFeeService.get_active_configuration()
        normal_rate = self.package.price / (self.package.duration_minutes or 1)

        if not config:
            return LateFeeService.calculate_late_fee(None, normal_rate, overdue_minutes)

        return LateFeeService.calculate_late_fee(config, normal_rate, overdue_minutes)

+     17:
+     18:     def get_all_revenue(self, filters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+     19:         """
+     20:         Get all revenue distributions across entire platform.
+     21:
+     22:         Args:
+     23:             filters: Dictionary containing filter parameters
+     24:
+     25:         Returns:
+     26:             Paginated revenue distributions with summary
+     27:         """
+     28:         # Parse date filters
+     29:         start_date = self._parse_date(filters.get('start_date'))
+     30:         end_date = self._parse_date(filters.get('end_date'))
+     31:
+     32:         # Parse boolean filters
+     33:         is_distributed = self._parse_bool(filters.get('is_distributed'))
+     34:         is_reversal = self._parse_bool(filters.get('is_reversal'))
+     35:         chargeghar_only = filters.get('chargeghar_only') == 'true'
+     36:
+     37:         # Get filtered queryset
+     38:         queryset = RevenueDistributionRepository.filter_distributions(
+     39:             station_id=filters.get('station_id'),
+     40:             franchise_id=filters.get('franchise_id'),
+     41:             vendor_id=filters.get('vendor_id'),
+     42:             chargeghar_only=chargeghar_only,
+     43:             start_date=start_date,
+     44:             end_date=end_date,
+     45:             is_distributed=is_distributed
+     46:         ).select_related(
+     47:             'transaction__user',
+     48:             'rental',
+     49:             'station',
+     50:             'franchise',
+     51:             'vendor'
+     52:         )
+     53:
+     54:         # Additional filters
+     55:         if filters.get('transaction_status'):
+     56:             queryset = queryset.filter(transaction__status=filters['transaction_status'])
+     57:
+     58:         if is_reversal is not None:
+     59:             queryset = queryset.filter(is_reversal=is_reversal)
+     60:
+     61:         # Calculate summary
+     62:         summary = queryset.aggregate(
+     63:             total_transactions=Count('id'),
+     64:             total_gross=Sum('gross_amount'),
+     65:             total_vat=Sum('vat_amount'),
+     66:             total_service_charge=Sum('service_charge'),
+     67:             total_net=Sum('net_amount'),
+     68:             total_chargeghar_share=Sum('chargeghar_share'),
+     69:             total_franchise_share=Sum('franchise_share'),
+     70:             total_vendor_share=Sum('vendor_share')
+     71:         )
+     72:
+     73:         # Handle None values in summary
+     74:         for key in summary:
+     75:             if summary[key] is None:
+     76:                 summary[key] = 0 if 'total_transactions' in key else Decimal('0')
+     77:
+     78:         # Paginate
+     79:         page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+     80:         page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+     81:         paginated = paginate_queryset(queryset, page, page_size)
+     82:
+     83:         # Format results
+     84:         paginated['results'] = [self._format_revenue_item(item) for item in paginated['results']]
+     85:         paginated['summary'] = summary
+     86:
+     87:         return paginated

+    136:     def _parse_date(self, date_str: str) -> date:
+    137:         """Parse date string to date object"""
+    138:         if not date_str:
+    139:             return None
+    140:         try:
+    141:             return date.fromisoformat(date_str)
+    142:         except (ValueError, AttributeError):
+    143:             return None
+    144:
+    145:     def _parse_bool(self, value: str) -> bool:
+    146:         """Parse boolean string"""
+    147:         if value is None:
+    148:             return None
+    149:         return value.lower() in ('true', '1', 'yes')

+      1: """
+      2: Admin IoT Monitoring Service
+      3: """
+      4: from typing import Dict, Any
+      5: from datetime import date
+      6:
+      7: from django.db.models import Count, Avg, Q
+      8:
+      9: from api.common.utils.helpers import paginate_queryset
+     10: from api.internal.models import IotSyncLog, StationStatusHistory
+     11:
+     12:
+     13: class AdminIoTMonitoringService:
+     14:     """Service for admin IoT monitoring operations"""
+     15:
+     16:     def get_iot_logs(self, log_type: str, filters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+     17:         """
+     18:         Get IoT logs based on type.
+     19:
+     20:         Args:
+     21:             log_type: 'sync' or 'history'
+     22:             filters: Filter parameters
+     23:
+     24:         Returns:
+     25:             Paginated logs with summary
+     26:         """
+     27:         if log_type == 'sync':
+     28:             return self._get_sync_logs(filters)
+     29:         elif log_type == 'history':
+     30:             return self._get_status_history(filters)
+     31:         else:
+     32:             raise ValueError(f"Invalid log_type: {log_type}. Must be 'sync' or 'history'")
+     33:
+     34:     def _get_sync_logs(self, filters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+     35:         """Get IoT sync logs"""
+     36:         queryset = IotSyncLog.objects.select_related('station').all()
+     37:
+     38:         # Apply filters
+     39:         if filters.get('station_id'):
+     40:             queryset = queryset.filter(station_id=filters['station_id'])
+     41:
+     42:         if filters.get('sync_type'):
+     43:             queryset = queryset.filter(sync_type=filters['sync_type'])
+     44:
+     45:         if filters.get('status'):
+     46:             queryset = queryset.filter(status=filters['status'])
+     47:
+     48:         if filters.get('start_date'):
+     49:             queryset = queryset.filter(created_at__date__gte=filters['start_date'])
+     50:
+     51:         if filters.get('end_date'):
+     52:             queryset = queryset.filter(created_at__date__lte=filters['end_date'])
+     53:
+     54:         # Calculate summary
+     55:         summary = queryset.aggregate(
+     56:             total_syncs=Count('id'),
+     57:             success_count=Count('id', filter=Q(status='SUCCESS')),
+     58:             failed_count=Count('id', filter=Q(status='FAILED')),
+     59:             avg_duration_ms=Avg('duration_ms')
+     60:         )
+     61:
+     62:         # Paginate
+     63:         page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+     64:         page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+     65:         paginated = paginate_queryset(queryset.order_by('-created_at'), page, page_size)
+     66:
+     67:         # Format results
+     68:         paginated['results'] = [self._format_sync_log(log) for log in paginated['results']]
+     69:         paginated['summary'] = summary
+     70:
+     71:         return paginated
+     72:
+     73:     def _get_status_history(self, filters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+     74:         """Get station status history"""
+     75:         queryset = StationStatusHistory.objects.select_related('station').all()
+     76:
+     77:         # Apply filters
+     78:         if filters.get('station_id'):
+     79:             queryset = queryset.filter(station_id=filters['station_id'])
+     80:
+     81:         if filters.get('status'):
+     82:             queryset = queryset.filter(status=filters['status'])
+     83:
+     84:         if filters.get('start_date'):
+     85:             queryset = queryset.filter(changed_at__date__gte=filters['start_date'])
+     86:
+     87:         if filters.get('end_date'):
+     88:             queryset = queryset.filter(changed_at__date__lte=filters['end_date'])
+     89:
+     90:         # Paginate
+     91:         page = int(filters.get('page', 1))
+     92:         page_size = int(filters.get('page_size', 20))
+     93:         paginated = paginate_queryset(queryset, page, page_size)
+     94:
+     95:         # Format results
+     96:         paginated['results'] = [self._format_status_history(history) for history in paginated['results']]
+     97:
+     98:         return paginated
+     99:
+    100:     def _format_sync_log(self, log: IotSyncLog) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    101:         """Format sync log for response"""
+    102:         return {
+    103:             'id': str(log.id),
+    104:             'created_at': log.created_at.isoformat(),
+    105:             'station_sn': log.station.serial_number,
+    106:             'station_name': log.station.station_name,
+    107:             'device_uuid': log.device_uuid,
+    108:             'sync_type': log.sync_type,
+    109:             'direction': log.direction,
+    110:             'status': log.status,
+    111:             'error_message': log.error_message,
+    112:             'duration_ms': log.duration_ms,
+    113:         }
+    114:
+    115:     def _format_status_history(self, history: StationStatusHistory) -> Dict[str, Any]:
+    116:         """Format status history for response"""
+    117:         return {
+    118:             'id': str(history.id),
+    119:             'changed_at': history.changed_at.isoformat(),
+    120:             'station_sn': history.station.serial_number,
+    121:             'station_name': history.station.station_name,
+    122:             'status': history.status,
+    123:             'previous_status': history.previous_status,
+    124:             'duration_seconds': history.duration_seconds,
+    125:             'triggered_by': history.triggered_by,
+    126:         }

+    34:     ],

+    36: )
+    37: class AdminIoTLogsView(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):

+    45:             log_type = request.query_params.get('type')
+    46:

+    52:                 'sync_type': request.query_params.get('sync_type'),
+    53:                 'status': request.query_params.get('status'),
+    54:                 'start_date': request.query_params.get('start_date'),
+    55:                 'end_date': request.query_params.get('end_date'),
+    56:                 'page': request.query_params.get('page', 1),
+    57:                 'page_size': request.query_params.get('page_size', 20),
+    58:             }
+    59:
+    60:             service = AdminIoTMonitoringService()
+    61:             return service.get_iot_logs(log_type, filters)
+    62:

+    64:             operation,
+    65:             "IoT logs retrieved successfully",

+    67:         )

+     57: **Location:** `api/user/rentals/models/battery_cycle_log.py` (NEW FILE)
+     58:
+     59: ```python
+     60: from django.db import models
+     61: from api.common.models import BaseModel
+     62:
+     63:
+     64: class BatteryCycleLog(BaseModel):
+     65:     """Track battery discharge cycles per rental"""
+     66:
+     67:     powerbank = models.ForeignKey(
+     68:         'stations.PowerBank',
+     69:         on_delete=models.CASCADE,
+     70:         related_name='cycle_logs'
+     71:     )
+     72:     rental = models.ForeignKey(
+     73:         'Rental',
+     74:         on_delete=models.CASCADE,
+     75:         related_name='cycle_logs'
+     76:     )
+     77:     start_level = models.IntegerField(help_text='Battery % at rental start')
+     78:     end_level = models.IntegerField(help_text='Battery % at return')
+     79:     discharge_percent = models.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=2, help_text='% discharged')
+     80:     cycle_contribution = models.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=4, help_text='Cycle count (0.XXXX)')
+     81:
+     82:     class Meta:
+     83:         db_table = 'battery_cycle_logs'
+     84:         verbose_name = 'Battery Cycle Log'
+     85:         verbose_name_plural = 'Battery Cycle Logs'
+     86:         indexes = [
+     87:             models.Index(fields=['powerbank', 'created_at']),
+     88:             models.Index(fields=['rental']),
+     89:         ]
+     90:
+     91:     def __str__(self):
+     92:         return f"{self.powerbank.serial_number} - {self.discharge_percent}% ({self.cycle_contribution} cycles)"
+     93: ```
+     94:

+    103:
+    104: ### PHASE 2: Service Layer
+    105:
+    106: #### 2.1 Create BatteryCycleService
+    107: **Location:** `api/user/rentals/services/battery_cycle_service.py` (NEW FILE)
+    108:
+    109: ```python
+    110: """
+    111: Battery Cycle Tracking Service
+    112: """
+    113: from decimal import Decimal
+    114: from typing import Optional
+    115:
+    116: from api.user.rentals.models import BatteryCycleLog
+    117: from api.user.stations.models import PowerBank
+    118:
+    119:
+    120: class BatteryCycleService:
+    121:     """Service for tracking battery cycles"""
+    122:
+    123:     @staticmethod
+    124:     def log_cycle(
+    125:         rental,
+    126:         powerbank: PowerBank,
+    127:         start_level: int,
+    128:         end_level: int
+    129:     ) -> Optional[BatteryCycleLog]:
+    130:         """
+    131:         Log battery cycle for a rental.
+    132:
+    133:         1 Cycle = 100% to 0% discharge
+    134:         Example: 100% → 30% = 0.70 cycles
+    135:
+    136:         Args:
+    137:             rental: Rental instance
+    138:             powerbank: PowerBank instance
+    139:             start_level: Battery % at start (0-100)
+    140:             end_level: Battery % at end (0-100)
+    141:
+    142:         Returns:
+    143:             BatteryCycleLog instance or None if no discharge
+    144:         """
+    145:         # Calculate discharge
+    146:         discharge_percent = max(0, start_level - end_level)
+    147:
+    148:         # Skip if no discharge (shouldn't happen but safety check)
+    149:         if discharge_percent == 0:
+    150:             return None
+    151:
+    152:         # Calculate cycle contribution (discharge / 100)
+    153:         cycle_contribution = Decimal(discharge_percent) / Decimal(100)
+    154:
+    155:         # Create log
+    156:         cycle_log = BatteryCycleLog.objects.create(
+    157:             powerbank=powerbank,
+    158:             rental=rental,
+    159:             start_level=start_level,
+    160:             end_level=end_level,
+    161:             discharge_percent=Decimal(discharge_percent),
+    162:             cycle_contribution=cycle_contribution
+    163:         )
+    164:
+    165:         # Update powerbank cumulative stats
+    166:         powerbank.total_cycles += cycle_contribution
+    167:         powerbank.total_rentals += 1
+    168:         powerbank.save(update_fields=['total_cycles', 'total_rentals', 'updated_at'])
+    169:
+    170:         return cycle_log
+    171:
+    172:     @staticmethod
+    173:     def check_5_minute_return(rental) -> bool:
+    174:         """
+    175:         Check if rental was returned within 5 minutes.
+    176:         Indicates potential hardware issue.
+    177:
+    178:         Args:
+    179:             rental: Rental instance with started_at and ended_at
+    180:
+    181:         Returns:
+    182:             True if returned within 5 minutes
+    183:         """
+    184:         if not rental.started_at or not rental.ended_at:
+    185:             return False
+    186:
+    187:         duration = rental.ended_at - rental.started_at
+    188:         return duration.total_seconds() < 300  # 5 minutes
+    189: ```
+    190:
+    191: #### 2.2 Update RentalService - Start Method
+    192: **Location:** `api/user/rentals/services/rental/start/*.py` (wherever start logic is)
+    193:
+    194: **Add to start method:**
+    195: ```python
+    196: # After powerbank is assigned and rental is created
+    197: if powerbank:
+    198:     rental.start_battery_level = powerbank.battery_level
+    199:     rental.save(update_fields=['start_battery_level'])
+    200: ```
+    201:
+    202: #### 2.3 Update RentalService - Return Method
+    203: **Location:** `api/user/rentals/services/rental/return_powerbank.py`
+    204:
+    205: **Add to return method:**
+    206: ```python

+    208:
+    209: # After rental.ended_at is set
+    210: rental.return_battery_level = return_battery_level  # from device/parameter
+    211:
+    212: # Check 5-minute rule
+    213: if BatteryCycleService.check_5_minute_return(rental):
+    214:     rental.is_under_5_min = True
+    215:     rental.hardware_issue_reported = True
+    216:     # TODO: Trigger admin notification (optional)
+    217:
+    218: rental.save(update_fields=['return_battery_level', 'is_under_5_min', 'hardware_issue_reported'])
+    219:
+    220: # Log battery cycle
+    221: if rental.start_battery_level and rental.return_battery_level:
+    222:     BatteryCycleService.log_cycle(
+    223:         rental=rental,
+    224:         powerbank=powerbank,
+    225:         start_level=rental.start_battery_level,
+    226:         end_level=rental.return_battery_level
+    227:     )
+    228: ```
+    229:

Track powerbank battery lifecycle:
  ✅ Battery levels at start/end
  ✅ Cycle count (1 cycle = 100% discharge)
  ✅ Hardware issues (5-minute returns)
  ✅ Total rental count per powerbank

📊 WHAT GETS TRACKED
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Per Rental:
  ✅ start_battery_level (e.g., 95%)
  ✅ return_battery_level (e.g., 45%)
  ✅ is_under_5_min (hardware issue indicator)
  ✅ hardware_issue_reported (flag for admin)

Per PowerBank:
  ✅ total_cycles (e.g., 45.7823 cycles)
  ✅ total_rentals (e.g., 127 rentals)

Per Cycle Log:
  ✅ Rental, PowerBank, Start/End levels
  ✅ Discharge % (e.g., 50%)
  ✅ Cycle contribution (e.g., 0.5000)
  ✅ Timestamp

🔧 BUSINESS LOGIC
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Battery Cycle Calculation:
  • 1 cycle = 100% → 0% discharge
  • 100% → 30% = 0.70 cycles
  • 80% → 50% = 0.30 cycles
  • Cumulative over powerbank lifetime

5-Minute Rule:
  • If duration < 5 minutes:
    - Set is_under_5_min = True
    - Set hardware_issue_reported = True
    - (Optional) Notify admin

When Tracking Happens:
  • Start: Capture start_battery_level
  • Return: Capture return_battery_level
  • Return: Calculate and log cycle
  • Return: Update powerbank stats
