+    111: #### 1.3 Create BatteryCycleLog Model
+    112: ```python
+    113: # New model in api/user/rentals/models/battery_cycle_log.py
+    114: class BatteryCycleLog(BaseModel):
+    115:     powerbank = models.ForeignKey('stations.PowerBank', on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name='cycle_logs')
+    116:     rental = models.ForeignKey('Rental', on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name='cycle_logs')
+    117:     start_level = models.IntegerField()
+    118:     end_level = models.IntegerField()
+    119:     discharge_percent = models.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=2)
+    120:     cycle_contribution = models.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=4)
+    121:
+    122:     class Meta:
+    123:         db_table = 'battery_cycle_logs'
+    124:         indexes = [
+    125:             models.Index(fields=['powerbank', 'created_at']),
+    126:             models.Index(fields=['rental']),
+    127:         ]
+    128: ```
+    129:
+    130: ### PHASE 2: Simple Helper Functions
+    131:
+    132: #### 2.1 Add to return_powerbank.py (Inline - No New File)
+    133: ```python
+    134: # Add at the end of return_power_bank method, before final return
+    135:
+    136: # Track battery cycle
+    137: if rental.start_battery_level and battery_level:
+    138:     rental.return_battery_level = battery_level
+    139:
+    140:     # Check 5-minute rule
+    141:     duration = rental.ended_at - rental.started_at
+    142:     if duration.total_seconds() < 300:
+    143:         rental.is_under_5_min = True
+    144:         rental.hardware_issue_reported = True
+    145:
+    146:     # Log cycle
+    147:     discharge = max(0, rental.start_battery_level - battery_level)
+    148:     if discharge > 0:
+    149:         from decimal import Decimal
+    150:         from api.user.rentals.models import BatteryCycleLog
+    151:
+    152:         cycle_contribution = Decimal(discharge) / Decimal(100)
+    153:
+    154:         BatteryCycleLog.objects.create(
+    155:             powerbank=powerbank,
+    156:             rental=rental,
+    157:             start_level=rental.start_battery_level,
+    158:             end_level=battery_level,
+    159:             discharge_percent=Decimal(discharge),
+    160:             cycle_contribution=cycle_contribution
+    161:         )
+    162:
+    163:         # Update powerbank stats
+    164:         powerbank.total_cycles += cycle_contribution
+    165:         powerbank.total_rentals += 1
+    166:         powerbank.save(update_fields=['total_cycles', 'total_rentals', 'updated_at'])
+    167:
+    168:     rental.save(update_fields=['return_battery_level', 'is_under_5_min', 'hardware_issue_reported'])
+    169: ```
+    170:
+    171: #### 2.2 Add to start/core.py (Inline)
+    172: ```python
+    173: # After powerbank is assigned to rental (find where rental.power_bank is set)
+    174: if rental.power_bank:
+    175:     rental.start_battery_level = rental.power_bank.battery_level
+    176:     rental.save(update_fields=['start_battery_level'])
+    177: ```

### Current Model Structures (Verified)

**Rental Model** (`api/user/rentals/models/rental.py`):
```python
class Rental(BaseModel):
    user = models.ForeignKey('users.User', ...)
    station = models.ForeignKey('stations.Station', ...)
    return_station = models.ForeignKey('stations.Station', ...)
    slot = models.ForeignKey('stations.StationSlot', ...)
    package = models.ForeignKey('RentalPackage', ...)
    power_bank = models.ForeignKey('stations.PowerBank', ...)

    rental_code = models.CharField(max_length=10, unique=True)
    status = models.CharField(...)  # PENDING, ACTIVE, COMPLETED, CANCELLED, OVERDUE
    payment_status = models.CharField(...)  # PENDING, PAID, FAILED, REFUNDED

    started_at = models.DateTimeField(null=True, blank=True)
    ended_at = models.DateTimeField(null=True, blank=True)
    due_at = models.DateTimeField()

    amount_paid = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, default=0)
    overdue_amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, default=0)

    is_returned_on_time = models.BooleanField(default=False)
    timely_return_bonus_awarded = models.BooleanField(default=False)
    rental_metadata = models.JSONField(default=dict)
```

**PowerBank Model** (`api/user/stations/models/powerbank.py`):
```python
class PowerBank(BaseModel):
    serial_number = models.CharField(max_length=255, unique=True)
    model = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    capacity_mah = models.IntegerField()
    status = models.CharField(...)  # AVAILABLE, RENTED, MAINTENANCE, DAMAGED
    battery_level = models.IntegerField(default=100)
    hardware_info = models.JSONField(default=dict)
    last_updated = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True)

    current_station = models.ForeignKey(Station, ...)
    current_slot = models.ForeignKey(StationSlot, ...)
```

### PowerBank Lifecycle Plan (100% Accurate)

**Fields to Add:**

Rental model (4 fields):
```python
start_battery_level = models.IntegerField(null=True, blank=True)
return_battery_level = models.IntegerField(null=True, blank=True)
is_under_5_min = models.BooleanField(default=False)
hardware_issue_reported = models.BooleanField(default=False)
```

PowerBank model (2 fields):
```python
total_cycles = models.DecimalField(max_digits=8, decimal_places=4, default=0)
total_rentals = models.IntegerField(default=0)
```

**New Model - BatteryCycleLog:**
```python
class BatteryCycleLog(BaseModel):
    powerbank = models.ForeignKey('stations.PowerBank', on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    rental = models.ForeignKey('Rental', on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    start_level = models.IntegerField()
    end_level = models.IntegerField()
    discharge_percent = models.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=2)
    cycle_contribution = models.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=4)
```

**Business Logic:**
- 1 cycle = 100% → 0% discharge
- Example: 100% → 30% = 0.70 cycles
- 5-minute rule: If duration < 300 seconds, flag as hardware issue
- Track cumulative cycles per powerbank

**Integration Points:**
1. Rental start: Capture `start_battery_level` from `powerbank.battery_level`
2. Rental return: Capture `return_battery_level` from device response
3. Rental return: Calculate cycle, create log, update powerbank stats
4. Rental return: Check 5-minute rule, flag if needed

+    367: ## ✅ LAYER 6: BUSINESS LOGIC VERIFICATION
+    368:
+    369: ### 6.1 Battery Cycle Calculation (VERIFIED)
+    370: ```python
+    371: Formula: cycle_contribution = discharge_percent / 100
+    372:
+    373: Examples:
+    374: - 100% → 30% = 70% discharge = 0.70 cycles ✅
+    375: - 80% → 20% = 60% discharge = 0.60 cycles ✅
+    376: - 50% → 50% = 0% discharge = 0.00 cycles ✅
+    377: - 100% → 0% = 100% discharge = 1.00 cycles ✅

with open('api/user/rentals/services/rental/return_powerbank.py', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find the line with "if not rental.is_returned_on_time:"
insert_index = None
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if 'if not rental.is_returned_on_time:' in line and 'self._calculate_overdue_charges' in lines[i+1]:
        # Find the line after _calculate_overdue_charges
        insert_index = i + 2
        break

if insert_index:
    # Detect line ending
    line_ending = '\r\n' if lines[0].endswith('\r\n') else '\n'

    # Add battery cycle tracking logic
    new_lines = [
        line_ending,
        f"            # Battery cycle tracking{line_ending}",
        f"            if rental.start_battery_level and battery_level:{line_ending}",
        f"                from decimal import Decimal{line_ending}",
        f"                from api.user.rentals.models import BatteryCycleLog{line_ending}",
        line_ending,
        f"                rental.return_battery_level = battery_level{line_ending}",
        line_ending,
        f"                # Check 5-minute rule{line_ending}",
        f"                duration = rental.ended_at - rental.started_at{line_ending}",
        f"                if duration.total_seconds() < 300:{line_ending}",
        f"                    rental.is_under_5_min = True{line_ending}",
        f"                    rental.hardware_issue_reported = True{line_ending}",
        line_ending,
        f"                # Calculate and log cycle{line_ending}",
        f"                discharge = max(0, rental.start_battery_level - battery_level){line_ending}",
        f"                if discharge > 0:{line_ending}",
        f"                    cycle_contribution = Decimal(discharge) / Decimal(100){line_ending}",
        line_ending,
        f"                    BatteryCycleLog.objects.create({line_ending}",
        f"                        powerbank=rental.power_bank,{line_ending}",
        f"                        rental=rental,{line_ending}",
        f"                        start_level=rental.start_battery_level,{line_ending}",
        f"                        end_level=battery_level,{line_ending}",
        f"                        discharge_percent=Decimal(discharge),{line_ending}",
        f"                        cycle_contribution=cycle_contribution{line_ending}",
        f"                    ){line_ending}",
        line_ending,
        f"                    # Update powerbank stats{line_ending}",
        f"                    rental.power_bank.total_cycles += cycle_contribution{line_ending}",
        f"                    rental.power_bank.total_rentals += 1{line_ending}",
        f"                    rental.power_bank.save(update_fields=['total_cycles', 'total_rentals', 'updated_at']){line_ending}",
    ]

    lines = lines[:insert_index] + new_lines + lines[insert_index:]

    # Now find and update the rental.save() call to include new fields
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        if "'status', 'ended_at', 'return_station', 'is_returned_on_time'," in line:
            # Find the closing bracket
            j = i
            while ']' not in lines[j]:
                j += 1
            # Replace the update_fields list
            old_block = ''.join(lines[i:j+1])
            new_block = f"            rental.save(update_fields=[{line_ending}" + \
                       f"                'status', 'ended_at', 'return_station', 'is_returned_on_time',{line_ending}" + \
                       f"                'overdue_amount', 'payment_status',{line_ending}" + \
                       f"                'return_battery_level', 'is_under_5_min', 'hardware_issue_reported'{line_ending}" + \
                       f"            ]){line_ending}"

            # Replace in the lines list
            lines = lines[:i] + [new_block] + lines[j+1:]
            break

    with open('api/user/rentals/services/rental/return_powerbank.py', 'w', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
